      <!-- Points Local Freeform v0.0.1 -->
      <div id="pointslocal-rail-search">
      </div>
      <script>
       (function(){
	var Freeform = {
		init: function () {
			console.log("Init Points Local v0.0.1");
			this.el = document.getElementById("pointslocal-rail-search") || false;
			if (this.el) {
				var isLoaded = this.el.getAttribute("data-loaded") || false;
				if (!isLoaded) {
					this.el.setAttribute("data-loaded", "1");
					this.addEvents();
				}
			}
		},
		addEvents: function() {
			['mousedown', 'scroll'].forEach(function (e) {
				window.addEventListener(e, function firstInteraction() {
					['mousedown', 'scroll'].forEach(function (e) {
						window.removeEventListener(e, firstInteraction, false);
					});
					Freeform.insertModule();
				}, false);
			});
		},
		insertModule: function() {
			console.log("Load Points Local");
			this.addLinkTag( "https://dist.pointslocal.com/pointslocal.widgets.min.css" );
			this.addScriptTag( "https://dist.pointslocal.com/pointslocal.widgets.min.js", function(){
				console.log("Run Points Local");
				var searchWidget = new Pointslocal('#pointslocal-rail-search', {
					widget: 'search',
					companion: { 
						'key': 'events',
						'widget': 'events', 
						'options': { 'count': 2, 'featured': 1 }
					},
					vars: { 
						'title': 'Local Events', 
						'container_class': 'pointslocal-widget'
					},
					stylesheet: 'hearst',
					template: 'pointslocal.search.mini'
				});
			});
		},
		addLinkTag: function (href) {
			var link = document.createElement('link');
			var head = document.head || document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
			link.rel = "stylesheet";
			link.type = "text/css";
			link.href = href;
			head.appendChild(link);
		},
		addScriptTag: function (src, callback) {
			var callback = callback || false;
			var script = document.createElement('script');
			var head = document.head || document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
			if (callback) {
				script.onload = callback;
			}
			script.src = src;
			head.appendChild(script);
		}
	};
	Freeform.init();
}());
      </script>
